<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каштан.html>кашта́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaštán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каштановый.html>кашта́новый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kaštánovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chestnut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каштановый.html>кашта́новая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:роща.html>ро́ща</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kaštánovaja</b> róšča</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>chestnut</b> grove</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>chestnut-colored, maroon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:каштановый.html>кашта́новые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kaštánovyje</b> vólosy</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>chestnut-colored/brown</b> hair</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***каяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:каяться.html>ка́яться</a> (9310)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kàjati</i> + reflexive <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каяться.html>ка́яться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kájatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покаяться.html>пока́яться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскаяться.html>раска́яться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to repent <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to feel sorrow or regret for what one has done or omitted to do</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to confess <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to admit to the truth, particularly in the context of sins or crimes committed</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<li>(no equivalent)</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскаиваться.html>раска́иваться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raskáivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ква.html>ква</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kva</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:квадратик.html>квадра́тик</a> (16765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квадрат.html>квадра́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kvadrát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квадратик.html>квадра́тик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kvadrátik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квадратик.html>квадра́тика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квадратик.html>квадра́тики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квадратик.html>квадра́тиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квадрат.html>квадра́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kvadrát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (small) square</li></ol>

***квалифицировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:квалифицировать.html>квалифици́ровать</a> (18539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">qualifizieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квалифицировать.html>квалифици́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kvalificírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to qualify</li>
<li>to qualify <i>(as)</i>, to categorize <i>(as)</i>, to consider <i>(as; to be)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:квалифицировать.html>квалифици́рую</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> аморальность</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>kvalificíruju</b> éto kak amoralʹnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I consider/regard this as immoral</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:квалифицировать.html>квалифици́ровать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деяние.html>дея́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:преступление.html>преступле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kvalificírovatʹ</b> dejánije kak prestuplénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to determine that the act is a crime</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:квалифицировать.html>квалифици́ровать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:преступление.html>преступле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kvalificírovatʹ</b> prestuplénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to determine the nature of the crime, categorize the crime</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́л</a> (3365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Quartal</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kvartál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>quarter <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a year</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>city block</li>
<li>quarter, district <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a city; in various expressions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:китайский.html>кита́йский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kitájskij <b>kvartál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Chinatown</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:латинский.html>лати́нский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">latínskij <b>kvartál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin_Quarter" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Latin Quarter">Latin Quarter</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фонарь.html>фонаре́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kvartál</b> krásnyx fonaréj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">red light district</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гей-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gej-<b>kvartál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gay district, gay village</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартальный.html>кварта́льный</a> (25639)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартал.html>кварта́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kvartál</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартальный.html>кварта́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kvartálʹnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>quarterly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in reference to a quarter of a year</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> city block
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:квартальный.html>кварта́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:планировка.html>планиро́вка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kvartálʹnaja</b> planiróvka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>city block</b> layout</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> urban ward <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in Russia until 1862</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:квартальный.html>кварта́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надзиратель.html>надзира́тель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kvartálʹnyj</b> nadzirátelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>urban ward</b> overseer</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартальный.html>кварта́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kvartálʹnyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартальный.html>кварта́льного</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартальный.html>кварта́льные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартальный.html>кварта́льных</a></b>)

***квартира.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ра</a> (354)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">quartarius</i>, via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Quartier</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kwartier</i> or, perhaps, Old <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kwartera</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kwatera</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kvartíra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́р</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>apartment, flat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">отде́лывать/<a href = vnd.unilang:отделать.html>отде́лать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ру</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdélyvatʹ/otdélatʹ <b>kvartíru</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to decorate <b>a flat</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">обставля́ть/<a href = vnd.unilang:обставить.html>обста́вить</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ру</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obstavljátʹ/obstávitʹ <b>kvartíru</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to furnish <b>a flat</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">переселя́ть/<a href = vnd.unilang:переселить.html>пересели́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вую</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ру</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pereseljátʹ/pereselítʹ na nóvuju <b>kvartíru</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move to a new place (of residence)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>quarters</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартирант.html>квартира́нт</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kvartiránt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kvartíra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́нт</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартирант.html>квартира́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kvartiránt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартирант.html>квартира́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартирант.html>квартира́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квартирант.html>квартира́нтов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">квартира́нтка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lodger, tenant, occupant</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> husband <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">spoken by his wife</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tenant of a communal apartment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> short-term convict <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually up to two years</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кварц.html>кварц</a> (31078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Quarz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кварц.html>кварц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kvarc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кварц.html>ква́рца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кварц.html>ква́рцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кварц.html>ква́рцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quartz</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="4" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">

***квас.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:квас.html>квас</a> (10250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">квасъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kvasŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kvasъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">leaven, fermented drink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квас.html>квас</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kvas</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квас.html>ква́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квас.html>квасы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:квас.html>квасо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">kvass</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a type of traditional fermented Russian no- or low-alcohol beverage, made from bread, often flavored with fruit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***кг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кг.html>кг</a> (7499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:килограмм.html>килогра́мм</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kilográmm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кг.html>кг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>kg, kilogram</li></ol>
